	O
Wide	O

Application	O
Services	O
(WAAS)	O
is	O
a	O
Cisco	Companies worked at
Systems	Companies worked at
technology	O
that	O

the	O
performance	O
of	O
applications	O
on	O
a	O
wide	O
area	O
network	O
(WAN).	O
WAAS	O

Cisco's	O
Wide	O

(WAFS-products	O

inside	O
of	O
a	O

applications	O
on	O
a	O
given	O
network.	O
	O
WAAS	O

of	O

traffic	O
over	O
your	O
network.	O

to	O
the	O
WAEs	O
so	O

can	O
act	O

client	O

and	O
the	O
destination	O
server.	O

application	O

to	O

traffic	O

to	O

your	O
